Actor K8Gore_TinyBlood {
  game Doom
  scale 0.2
  speed 7
  health 1
  radius 8
  height 1
  +DontSplash
  Gravity 0.1 //0.7
  Decal K8GoreBloodSplat
  +MISSILE
  +CLIENTSIDEONLY
  +NOTELEPORT
  +NOBLOCKMAP
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  -EXPLODEONWATER
  +DOOMBOUNCE
  BounceFactor 0.01

  States {
    Spawn:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(waterlevel > 1, "Splash")
      BLUX A 500
      Stop

    NoSpawn:
      TNT1 A 0
      Stop

    Splash:
      BLOD A 0
      TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("K8Gore_Underblood1", 7, 0, random(0, 360), 2, random(30, 150))
      Stop

    Death:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("blooddrop3")
      XDT1 EFGHIJKL 2
      Stop
  }
}


Actor K8Gore_Blood Replaces Blood {
  Decal K8GoreBloodSplat
  game Doom
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  +NOGRAVITY
  +THRUACTORS
  +CLIENTSIDEONLY
  -ALLOWPARTICLES
  Scale 0.5
  Speed 0

  States {
    Spawn:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(waterlevel > 1, "Splash")
      TNT1 AAAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("K8Gore_FlyingBloodFake", 0, 0, random(0, 360), 2, random(0, 90))
      TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("K8Gore_FlyingBloodLevel3", 7, 0, random(0, 360), 2, random(40, 60))
      TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("K8Gore_FlyingBlood", 7, 0, random(0, 360), 2, random(20, 40))
      TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("K8Gore_BloodmistSmall", 0, 0, random(0, 360), 2, random(10, 40))
      //TNT1 AA 0 A_CustomMissile("SuperGoreMistTiny", 0, 0, random(0, 360), 2, random(60, 90))
      TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("K8Gore_BloodHit", 0, 0, random(0, 360), 2, random(0, 90))
      Stop

    Splash:
      BLOD A 0
      TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("K8Gore_Underblood1", 7, 0, random(0, 360), 2, random(30, 150))
      Stop

    Spray:
      Goto Spawn
  }
}


Actor K8Gore_BloodHit {
  height 8

  +NOBLOCKMAP
  +NOGRAVITY

Actor K8Gore_FlyingBlood {
  game Doom
  scale 0.5
  speed 4
  health 1
  radius 8
  height 1
  Gravity 0.1 //0.8
  damage 0
  Renderstyle Translucent
  Alpha 0.95
  DamageType Blood
  Decal K8GoreBloodSuper
  +MISSILE
  +CLIENTSIDEONLY
  +NOTELEPORT
  +NOBLOCKMAP
  +THRUACTORS
  +BLOODLESSIMPACT
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  +NODAMAGETHRUST
  +MOVEWITHSECTOR
  +CORPSE
  -DONTSPLASH
  Mass 5 //1

  States {
    Spawn:
      TNT1 A 0
      //BLOD ABCD 2
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(waterlevel > 1, "Splash")
      BLOD AB 2
      TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(waterlevel > 1, "Splash")
      TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(255, "Spawn1", "Spawn2")

    Spawn1:
      BLOD C 1
      TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(waterlevel > 1, "Splash")
      Loop

    Spawn2:
      BLOD E 1
      TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(waterlevel > 1, "Splash")
      Loop

    Splash:
      BLOD A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("K8Gore_Underblood2")
      Stop

    Death:
      TNT1 A 0
      //TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("SmallBloodSplasher", 0, 0, random(0, 360), 2, random(0, 160))
      TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("blooddrop2")
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("K8Gore_BloodSpot", 0, 1)
      //TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("K8Gore_CeilBloodChecker", -15, 0, 90, 2, 90)
      TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("K8Gore_DetectCeilBloodSimpler",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
      //TNT1 AAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("K8Gore_BloodTr255", 0, 0, random(0, 360), 2, random(0, 360))
      TNT1 A 1
      Stop
   }
}


Actor K8Gore_FlyingBloodMuchFaster : K8Gore_FlyingBlood {
  speed 8
}


Actor K8Gore_FlyingBloodLevel3 : K8Gore_FlyingBlood {
  Scale 1.0
  Speed 5 //7
  Mass 5 //1
}


Actor K8Gore_BloodSpot {
  game Doom
  radius 2
  height 2
  mass 1
  Health 300
  +NOTELEPORT
  +CLIENTSIDEONLY
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  +MOVEWITHSECTOR
  +FLOORCLIP
  +NOTARGET
  -SHOOTABLE
  +NOBLOOD
  -DONTSPLASH
  -SOLID
  +THRUACTORS
  Renderstyle Translucent
  Alpha 0.9
  Mass 99999999
  Scale 0.5
  Decal K8GoreBloodSplat
  DamageFactor "TeleportRemover", 100.0

  States {
    Spawn:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_LayToFloorWithYaw(Random(0, 360))
      //TNT1 A 0 A_SetRollExt(0)
      //TNT1 A 0 A_SetYawExt(Random(0, 360))
      //TNT1 A 0 A_SetPitchExt(0)
      TNT1 A 0 A_SetScaleXExt(Random(3, 9)/10.0)
      TNT1 A 0 A_CheckFloorTextureGlob("*water*", "SplashWater", AAPTR_DEFAULT, false)
      TNT1 A 0 A_CheckFloorTextureGlob("*nukage*", "SplashWater", AAPTR_DEFAULT, false)
      TNT1 A 0 A_CheckFloorTextureGlob("*lava*", "SplashWater", AAPTR_DEFAULT, false)
      TNT1 A 0 A_CheckFloorTextureGlob("*blood*", "SplashWater", AAPTR_DEFAULT, false)
      TNT1 A 0 A_CheckFloorTextureGlob("*slime*", "SplashWater", AAPTR_DEFAULT, false)
      TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(waterlevel > 1, "SplashWater")
      //TNT1 A 0 A_CheckFloor("SpawnNormally")
      //Goto Splash

    SpawnNormally:
      //TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("GibRemoving")
      TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(255, "SpawnBFrameOnly", "SpawnCFrameOnly", "SpawnDFrameOnly")

    SpawnAFrameOnly:
      BPDL A 800 //duration
      Loop

    SpawnBFrameOnly:
      BPDL B 800 //duration
      Loop

    SpawnCFrameOnly:
      BPDL C 800 //duration
      Loop

    SpawnDFrameOnly:
      BPDL D 800 //duration
      Loop

    FadeA:
      //TNT1 A 0
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      TNT1 A 0 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeB:
      //TNT1 A 0
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      TNT1 A 0 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeC:
      //TNT1 A 0
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      TNT1 A 0 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeD:
      //TNT1 A 0
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      TNT1 A 0 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    Splash:
      TNT1 A 0 //A_k8ConLog("SPLASH SLPASH!")
      //BLOD A 0
      //Stop
      Goto SpawnNormally

    SplashWater:
      //TNT1 A 0 A_k8ConLog("SPLASH SLPASH IN WATER!")
      TNT1 A 0 A_FadeOut(0.3)
      TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(255, "SpawnBFrameOnlyWater", "SpawnCFrameOnlyWater", "SpawnDFrameOnlyWater")

    SpawnAFrameOnlyWater:
      BPDL A random(50, 100) //duration
      Goto FadeAWater

    SpawnBFrameOnlyWater:
      BPDL B random(50, 100) //duration
      Goto FadeBWater

    SpawnCFrameOnlyWater:
      BPDL C random(50, 100) //duration
      Goto FadeCWater

    SpawnDFrameOnlyWater:
      BPDL D random(50, 100) //duration
      Goto FadeDWater

    FadeAWater:
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      TNT1 A 0 A_FadeOut(0.05)
      Loop

    FadeBWater:
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      TNT1 A 0 A_FadeOut(0.05)
      Loop

    FadeCWater:
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      TNT1 A 0 A_FadeOut(0.05)
      Loop

    FadeDWater:
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      TNT1 A 0 A_FadeOut(0.05)
      Loop

    Death:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
      Stop
  }
}

// Checks if there is a ceiling above, and isn't hitting a monster.
Actor K8Gore_CeilBloodChecker : K8Gore_FlyingBlood {
  +THRUACTORS
  +BLOODLESSIMPACT
  damagetype Blood
  damage 0
  Radius 0
  Height 0
  Speed 400
  Gravity 0.0
  Decal K8GoreBloodSuper

  States {
    Spawn:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(waterlevel > 1, "Splash")
      TNT1 A 4
      Stop

    Splash:
      BLOD A 0
      Stop

    Death:
      TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItem("K8Gore_CeilBloodSpot",0,0,0,1)
      TNT1 A 5
      Stop

    Xdeath:
      TNT1 A 1
      Stop
  }
}


Actor K8Gore_CeilBloodCheckerLarge : K8Gore_CeilBloodChecker {
  States {
    Death:
      TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItem("K8Gore_CeilBloodSpotLarge",0,0,0,1)
      TNT1 A 5
      Stop
  }
}


// The Ceil Blood Spot.

  +CEILINGHUGGER

      BPDL AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 2 ThrustThingZ(0,300,0,1)
      BPDL AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 2 ThrustThingZ(0,300,0,1)
      BPDL AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 2 ThrustThingZ(0,300,0,1)
      BPDL AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 2 ThrustThingZ(0,300,0,1)
      BPDL AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 2 ThrustThingZ(0,300,0,1)
      BPDL AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 2 ThrustThingZ(0,300,0,1)
      BPDL AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 2 ThrustThingZ(0,300,0,1)
      BPDL AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 2 ThrustThingZ(0,300,0,1)
      BPDL AAAAAAAAA 1 A_FadeOut(0.1)
      Stop
  }
}

Actor K8Gore_MinuscleBloodSpot : K8Gore_BloodSpot {
  game Doom
  radius 2
  height 2
  mass 1
  Health 300
  +NOTELEPORT
  +CLIENTSIDEONLY
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  +MOVEWITHSECTOR
  +FLOORCLIP
  +NOTARGET
  -SHOOTABLE
  +NOBLOOD
  -DONTSPLASH
  -SOLID
  +THRUACTORS
  Alpha 0.9
  Mass 99999999
  Scale 0.25
  Decal K8GoreBloodSplat
  DamageFactor "TeleportRemover", 100.0

  States {
    Spawn:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(waterlevel > 1, "Splash")
      TNT1 A 1
      TNT1 A 0 A_CheckFloor("SpawnNormally")
      Goto Splash

    SpawnNormally:
      TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(255, "SpawnBFrameOnly", "SpawnCFrameOnly", "SpawnDFrameOnly")

    SpawnAFrameOnly:
      BPDL A 800 //duration
      Goto FadeA

    SpawnBFrameOnly:
      BPDL B 800 //duration
      Goto FadeB

    SpawnCFrameOnly:
      BPDL C 800 //duration
      Goto FadeC

    SpawnDFrameOnly:
      BPDL D 800 //duration
      Goto FadeD

    FadeA:
      BPDL AAAA 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeB:
      BPDL BBBB 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeC:
      BPDL CCCC 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeD:
      BPDL DDDD 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    Splash:
      BLOD AAAAA 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    Death:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
      Stop
  }
}

      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(waterlevel > 1, "Splash")
      TNT1 A 0 A_LayToFloorWithYaw(Random(0, 360))
      //TNT1 A 0 A_SetRollExt(0)
      //TNT1 A 0 A_SetYawExt(Random(0, 360))
      //TNT1 A 0 A_SetPitchExt(0)
      TNT1 A 0 A_SetScaleXExt(Random(6, 12)/10.0)
      TNT5 A 1
      TNT1 A 0 //A_SpawnItemEx("K8Gore_BootSmearerRed",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
      TNT5 A 30
      TNT5 BCD 5
      TNT5 EFGHIJKLMNOP 5
      TNT5 QRSTUVWXYZ 5

    Live:
      TNT5 Z 900 //duration
      /*
      TNT1 A 0 {
        if (GetCVar("k8GoreBloodTransient") != 0) { return state("Splash"); }
        return state("Live");
      }
      */
      Loop

    Splash:
      BLOD A 0
      Stop
  }
}

      TNT1 A 0 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeB:

      Loop

    FadeD:
      //TNT1 A 0
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)

    SpawnAFrameOnlyWater:
      BPDL A random(50, 100) //duration
      Goto FadeAWater

    SpawnBFrameOnlyWater:
      BPDL B random(50, 100) //duration
      Goto FadeBWater

    SpawnCFrameOnlyWater:
      BPDL C random(50, 100) //duration
      Goto FadeCWater

    SpawnDFrameOnlyWater:
      BPDL D random(50, 100) //duration
      Goto FadeDWater

      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      TNT1 A 0 A_FadeOut(0.05)
      Loop

    Death:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
      Stop
  }

Actor K8Gore_MinuscleBloodSpotTransient : K8Gore_BloodSpotTransient {
  game Doom
  radius 2
  height 2
  mass 1
  Health 300
  +NOTELEPORT
  +CLIENTSIDEONLY
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  +MOVEWITHSECTOR
  +FLOORCLIP
  +NOTARGET
  -SHOOTABLE
  +NOBLOOD
  -DONTSPLASH
  -SOLID
  +THRUACTORS
  Alpha 0.9
  Mass 99999999
  Scale 0.25
  Decal K8GoreBloodSplatTransient
  DamageFactor "TeleportRemover", 100.0

  States {
    Spawn:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(waterlevel > 1, "Splash")
      TNT1 A 1
      TNT1 A 0 A_CheckFloor("SpawnNormally")
      Goto Splash

    SpawnNormally:
      TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(255, "SpawnBFrameOnly", "SpawnCFrameOnly", "SpawnDFrameOnly")

    SpawnAFrameOnly:
      BPDL A 800 //duration
      Goto FadeA

    SpawnBFrameOnly:
      BPDL B 800 //duration
      Goto FadeB

    SpawnCFrameOnly:
      BPDL C 800 //duration
      Goto FadeC

    SpawnDFrameOnly:
      BPDL D 800 //duration
      Goto FadeD

    FadeA:
      BPDL AAAA 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeB:
      BPDL BBBB 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeC:
      BPDL CCCC 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeD:
      BPDL DDDD 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    Splash:
      BLOD AAAAA 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    Death:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
      Stop
  }
}

      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      TNT1 A 0 A_FadeOut(0.01)

    FadeB:

    SpawnAFrameOnlyWater:

      Goto FadeAWater

    SpawnBFrameOnlyWater:

      Goto FadeBWater

    SpawnCFrameOnlyWater:

      Goto FadeCWater

      Loop

      TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
      Stop
  }

Actor K8Gore_MinuscleBloodSpotGreen : K8Gore_BloodSpotGreen {
  Translation "16:48=112:127", "64:79=112:127", "164:167=117:127", "168:191=112:127", "232:235=119:127", "236:239=123:127"
  game Doom
  radius 2
  height 2
  mass 1
  Health 300
  +NOTELEPORT
  +CLIENTSIDEONLY
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  +MOVEWITHSECTOR
  +FLOORCLIP
  +NOTARGET
  -SHOOTABLE
  +NOBLOOD
  -DONTSPLASH
  -SOLID
  +THRUACTORS
  Alpha 0.9
  Mass 99999999
  Scale 0.25
  Decal K8GoreBloodSplatGreen
  DamageFactor "TeleportRemover", 100.0

  States {
    Spawn:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(waterlevel > 1, "Splash")
      TNT1 A 1
      TNT1 A 0 A_CheckFloor("SpawnNormally")
      Goto Splash

    SpawnNormally:
      TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(255, "SpawnBFrameOnly", "SpawnCFrameOnly", "SpawnDFrameOnly")

    SpawnAFrameOnly:
      BPDL A 800 //duration
      Goto FadeA

    SpawnBFrameOnly:
      BPDL B 800 //duration
      Goto FadeB

    SpawnCFrameOnly:
      BPDL C 800 //duration
      Goto FadeC

    SpawnDFrameOnly:
      BPDL D 800 //duration
      Goto FadeD

    FadeA:
      BPDL AAAA 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeB:
      BPDL BBBB 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeC:
      BPDL CCCC 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeD:
      BPDL DDDD 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    Splash:
      BLOD AAAAA 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    Death:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
      Stop
  }
}

      BPDL C 800 //duration
      Goto FadeC

    SpawnDFrameOnly:
      BPDL D 800 //duration
      Goto FadeD

    FadeA:
      BPDL AAAA 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeB:
      BPDL BBBB 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeC:
      BPDL CCCC 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeD:
      BPDL DDDD 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    Splash:
      BLOD AAAAA 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    Death:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
      Stop
  }
}

      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      TNT1 A 0 A_FadeOut(0.01)

      Loop

    FadeD:
      //TNT1 A 0
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)

      Loop

    Splash:
      TNT1 A 0 //A_k8ConLog("SPLASH SLPASH!")
      //BLOD A 0
      //Stop
      Goto SpawnNormally

    SplashWater:
      //TNT1 A 0 A_k8ConLog("SPLASH SLPASH IN WATER!")
      TNT1 A 0 A_FadeOut(0.3)
      TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(255, "SpawnBFrameOnlyWater", "SpawnCFrameOnlyWater", "SpawnDFrameOnlyWater")

    SpawnAFrameOnlyWater:
      BPDL A random(50, 100) //duration
      Goto FadeAWater

    SpawnBFrameOnlyWater:
      BPDL B random(50, 100) //duration
      Goto FadeBWater

    SpawnCFrameOnlyWater:
      BPDL C random(50, 100) //duration
      Goto FadeCWater

    SpawnDFrameOnlyWater:
      BPDL D random(50, 100) //duration
      Goto FadeDWater

    FadeAWater:
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL AAAA 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)

      TNT1 A 0 A_FadeOut(0.05)
      Loop

    FadeBWater:
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL BBBB 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)

      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL CCCC 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      TNT1 A 0 A_FadeOut(0.05)
      Loop

    FadeDWater:

      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      BPDL DDDD 1 //A_ChangeScaleXExt(-0.001, 0.05)
      TNT1 A 0 A_FadeOut(0.05)
      Loop

    Death:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
      Stop
  }
}

Actor K8Gore_MinuscleBloodSpotBlue : K8Gore_BloodSpotBlue {
  Translation "16:48=240:247", "64:79=240:247", "164:167=201:207", "168:191=192:207", "232:235=100:207", "236:239=199:207"
  game Doom
  radius 2
  height 2
  mass 1
  Health 300
  +NOTELEPORT
  +CLIENTSIDEONLY
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  +MOVEWITHSECTOR
  +FLOORCLIP
  +NOTARGET
  -SHOOTABLE
  +NOBLOOD
  -DONTSPLASH
  -SOLID
  +THRUACTORS
  Alpha 0.9
  Mass 99999999
  Scale 0.25
  Decal K8GoreBloodSplatBlue
  DamageFactor "TeleportRemover", 100.0

  States {
    Spawn:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(waterlevel > 1, "Splash")
      TNT1 A 1
      TNT1 A 0 A_CheckFloor("SpawnNormally")
      Goto Splash

    SpawnNormally:
      TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(255, "SpawnBFrameOnly", "SpawnCFrameOnly", "SpawnDFrameOnly")

    SpawnAFrameOnly:
      BPDL A 800 //duration
      Goto FadeA

    SpawnBFrameOnly:
      BPDL B 800 //duration
      Goto FadeB

    SpawnCFrameOnly:
      BPDL C 800 //duration
      Goto FadeC

    SpawnDFrameOnly:
      BPDL D 800 //duration
      Goto FadeD

    FadeA:
      BPDL AAAA 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeB:
      BPDL BBBB 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeC:
      BPDL CCCC 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeD:
      BPDL DDDD 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    Splash:
      BLOD AAAAA 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    Death:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
      Stop
  }
}

  height 2

  Health 300

  +CLIENTSIDEONLY
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  +MOVEWITHSECTOR
  +FLOORCLIP
  +NOTARGET
  -SHOOTABLE
  +NOBLOOD
  -DONTSPLASH
  -SOLID

  Alpha 0.9

  Decal K8GoreBloodSplatTransient_Blue

  States {
    Spawn:
      TNT1 A 0

      TNT1 A 1
      TNT1 A 0 A_CheckFloor("SpawnNormally")

    SpawnNormally:
      TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(255, "SpawnBFrameOnly", "SpawnCFrameOnly", "SpawnDFrameOnly")

    SpawnAFrameOnly:
      BPDL A 800 //duration
      Goto FadeA

    SpawnBFrameOnly:
      BPDL B 800 //duration
      Goto FadeB

    SpawnCFrameOnly:
      BPDL C 800 //duration
      Goto FadeC

    SpawnDFrameOnly:
      BPDL D 800 //duration
      Goto FadeD

    FadeA:
      BPDL AAAA 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeB:
      BPDL BBBB 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeC:
      BPDL CCCC 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    FadeD:
      BPDL DDDD 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    Splash:
      BLOD AAAAA 1 A_FadeOut(0.01)
      Loop

    Death:
      TNT1 A 0
      TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
      Stop
  }
